   637	fn write_grouped_arguments<'a>(
   638	    node: &AstNode<'a, ArenaVec<'a, Argument<'a>>>,
   639	    group_layout: GroupedCallArgumentLayout,
   640	    f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>,
   641	) {
   642	    let last_index = node.len() - 1;
   643	    let only_one_argument = last_index == 0;
   644	    let mut non_grouped_breaks = false;
   645	    let mut grouped_breaks = false;
   646	    let mut has_cached = false;
   647	
   648	    // Pre-format the arguments to determine if they can be grouped.
   649	    let elements = node
   650	        .iter()
   651	        .enumerate()
   652	        .map(|(index, argument)| {
   653	            let is_grouped_argument = (group_layout.is_grouped_first() && index == 0)
   654	                || (group_layout.is_grouped_last() && index == last_index);
   655	
   656	            // We have to get the lines before the argument has been formatted, because it relies on
   657	            // the comments before the argument. After formatting, the comments might marked as printed,
   658	            // which would lead to a wrong line count.
   659	            let lines_before = f.source_text().get_lines_before(argument.span(), f.comments());
   660	            let comma = (last_index != index).then_some(",");
   661	
   662	            let interned = f.intern(&format_once(|f| {
   663	                if is_grouped_argument {
   664	                    match argument.as_ast_nodes() {
   665	                        AstNodes::Function(function)
   666	                            if !group_layout.is_grouped_first()
   667	                                && (!only_one_argument
   668	                                    || function_has_only_simple_parameters(&function.params)) =>
   669	                        {
   670	                            has_cached = true;
   671	                            return write!(
   672	                                f,
   673	                                [
   674	                                    FormatFunction::new_with_options(
   675	                                        function,
   676	                                        FormatFunctionOptions {
   677	                                            cache_mode: FunctionCacheMode::Cache,
   678	                                            ..FormatFunctionOptions::default()
   679	                                        },
   680	                                    ),
   681	                                    comma
   682	                                ]
   683	                            );
   684	                        }
   685	                        AstNodes::ArrowFunctionExpression(arrow) => {
   686	                            has_cached = true;
   687	                            return write!(
   688	                                f,
   689	                                [
   690	                                    FormatJsArrowFunctionExpression::new_with_options(
   691	                                        arrow,
   692	                                        FormatJsArrowFunctionExpressionOptions {
   693	                                            cache_mode: FunctionCacheMode::Cache,
   694	                                            ..FormatJsArrowFunctionExpressionOptions::default()
   695	                                        },
   696	                                    ),
   697	                                    comma
   698	                                ]
   699	                            );
   700	                        }
   701	                        _ => {}
   702	                    }
   703	                }
   704	                write!(f, [argument, comma]);
   705	            }));
   706	
   707	            let break_type =
   708	                if is_grouped_argument { &mut grouped_breaks } else { &mut non_grouped_breaks };
   709	
   710	            *break_type = *break_type || interned.as_ref().is_some_and(FormatElement::will_break);
   711	
   712	            (interned, lines_before)
   713	        })
   714	        .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   715	
   716	    // If any of the not grouped elements break, then fall back to the variant where
   717	    // all arguments are printed in expanded mode.
   718	    if non_grouped_breaks {
   719	        return format_all_elements_broken_out(node, elements.into_iter(), true, f);
   720	    }
   721	
   722	    // First write the most expanded variant because it needs `arguments`.
   723	    let most_expanded = {
   724	        let mut buffer = VecBuffer::new(f.state_mut());
   725	        buffer.write_element(FormatElement::Tag(Tag::StartEntry));
   726	
   727	        format_all_elements_broken_out(node, elements.iter().cloned(), true, &mut buffer);
   728	
   729	        buffer.write_element(FormatElement::Tag(Tag::EndEntry));
   730	
   731	        buffer.into_vec().into_bump_slice()
   732	    };
   733	
   734	    // Now reformat the first or last argument if they happen to be a function or arrow function expression.
   735	    // Function and arrow function expression apply a custom formatting that removes soft line breaks from the parameters,
   736	    // type parameters, and return type annotation.
   737	    //
   738	    // This implementation caches the function body of the "normal" formatted function or arrow function expression
   739	    // to avoid quadratic complexity if the functions' body contains another call expression with an arrow or function expression
   740	    // as first or last argument.
   741	    let mut grouped = elements;
   742	    if has_cached {
   743	        let (argument, grouped_element) = match group_layout {
   744	            GroupedCallArgumentLayout::GroupedFirstArgument => {
   745	                (node.first().unwrap(), &mut grouped.first_mut().unwrap().0)
   746	            }
   747	            GroupedCallArgumentLayout::GroupedLastArgument => {
   748	                (node.last().unwrap(), &mut grouped.last_mut().unwrap().0)
   749	            }
   750	        };
   751	
   752	        let function_params = match argument.as_ast_nodes() {
   753	            AstNodes::ArrowFunctionExpression(arrow) => Some(&arrow.params),
   754	            AstNodes::Function(function) => Some(&function.params),
   755	            _ => None,
   756	        };
   757	
   758	        // Turns out, using the grouped layout isn't a good fit because some parameters of the
   759	        // grouped function or arrow expression break. In that case, fall back to the all args expanded
   760	        // formatting.
   761	        // This back tracking is required because testing if the grouped argument breaks would also return `true`
   762	        // if any content of the function body breaks. But, as far as this is concerned, it's only interested if
   763	        // any content in the signature breaks.
   764	        //
   765	        // <https://github.com/biomejs/biome/blob/98ca2ae9f3b9b25a14d63b243223583aba6e4907/crates/biome_js_formatter/src/js/expressions/call_arguments.rs#L466-L482>
   766	        if let Some(params) = function_params {
   767	            let Some(cached_element) = f.context().get_cached_element(params.as_ref()) else {
   768	                unreachable!(
   769	                    "The parameters should have already been formatted and cached in the `FormatFunction` or `FormatJsArrowFunctionExpression`"
   770	                );
   771	            };
   772	
   773	            // For decorated function patterns like `decorator("name")((props: {...}) => {...})`,
   774	            // the arrow function should be kept hugged even if its signature breaks.
   775	            // <https://github.com/prettier/prettier/blob/0273e33fc691e28e4ab3f3c8ee86918b65cf823d/src/language-js/print/function-parameters.js#L241-L292>
   776	            let is_decorated = is_decorated_function(argument);
   777	
   778	            // Remove soft lines from the cached parameters and check if they would break.
   779	            // If they break even without soft lines, we need to use the expanded layout.
   780	            // However, decorated functions are allowed to break while staying hugged.
   781	            let interned = f.intern(&format_once(|f| {
   782	                RemoveSoftLinesBuffer::new(f).write_element(cached_element);
   783	            }));
   784	
   785	            if let Some(interned) = interned {
   786	                if interned.will_break() && !is_decorated {
   787	                    return format_all_elements_broken_out(node, grouped.into_iter(), true, f);
   788	                }
   789	
   790	                // No break; it should print the element without soft lines.
   791	                // It would be used in the `FormatFunction` or `FormatJsArrowFunctionExpression`.
   792	                // For decorated functions, we keep the original cached element (with soft lines)
   793	                // so the parameters can break while staying hugged.
   794	                if !is_decorated {
   795	                    f.context_mut().cache_element(params.as_ref(), interned);
   796	                }
   797	            }
   798	        }
   799	
   800	        *grouped_element = if group_layout.is_grouped_first() {
   801	            f.intern(&format_with(|f| {
   802	                FormatGroupedFirstArgument { argument }.fmt(f);
   803	                write!(f, (last_index != 0).then_some(","));
   804	            }))
   805	        } else {
   806	            f.intern(&FormatGroupedLastArgument { argument, is_only: only_one_argument })
   807	        }
   808	    }
   809	
   810	    // Write the second variant that forces the group of the first/last argument to expand.
   811	    let middle_variant = {
   812	        let mut buffer = VecBuffer::new(f.state_mut());
   813	
   814	        buffer.write_element(FormatElement::Tag(Tag::StartEntry));
   815	
   816	        write!(
   817	            buffer,
   818	            [
   819	                "(",
   820	                format_with(|f| {
   821	                    let mut joiner = f.join_with(soft_line_break_or_space());
   822	
   823	                    for (i, (element, _)) in grouped.iter().enumerate() {
   824	                        if (group_layout.is_grouped_first() && i == 0)
   825	                            || (group_layout.is_grouped_last() && i == last_index)
   826	                        {
   827	                            joiner.entry(
   828	                                &group(&format_with(|f| {
   829	                                    if let Some(arg_element) = element.clone() {
   830	                                        f.write_element(arg_element);
   831	                                    }
   832	                                }))
   833	                                .should_expand(true),
   834	                            );
   835	                        } else {
   836	                            joiner.entry(&format_with(|f| {
   837	                                if let Some(arg_element) = element.clone() {
   838	                                    f.write_element(arg_element);
   839	                                }
   840	                            }));
   841	                        }
   842	                    }
   843	                }),
   844	                ")"
   845	            ]
   846	        );
   847	
   848	        buffer.write_element(FormatElement::Tag(Tag::EndEntry));
   849	
   850	        buffer.into_vec().into_bump_slice()
   851	    };
   852	
   853	    // If the grouped content breaks, then we can skip the most_flat variant,
   854	    // since we already know that it won't be fitting on a single line.
   855	    let variants = if grouped_breaks {
   856	        write!(f, [expand_parent()]);
   857	        ArenaVec::from_array_in([middle_variant, most_expanded], f.context().allocator())
   858	    } else {
   859	        // Write the most flat variant with the first or last argument grouped.
   860	        let most_flat = {
   861	            let mut buffer = VecBuffer::new(f.state_mut());
   862	            buffer.write_element(FormatElement::Tag(Tag::StartEntry));
   863	
   864	            write!(
   865	                buffer,
   866	                [
   867	                    "(",
   868	                    format_once(|f| {
   869	                        f.join_with(soft_line_break_or_space()).entries(grouped.into_iter().map(
   870	                            |(element, _)| {
   871	                                format_once(move |f| {
   872	                                    if let Some(element) = element {
   873	                                        f.write_element(element);
   874	                                    }
   875	                                })
   876	                            },
   877	                        ));
   878	                    }),
   879	                    ")",
   880	                ]
   881	            );
   882	
   883	            buffer.write_element(FormatElement::Tag(Tag::EndEntry));
   884	
   885	            buffer.into_vec().into_bump_slice()
   886	        };
   887	
   888	        ArenaVec::from_array_in([most_flat, middle_variant, most_expanded], f.context().allocator())
   889	    };
   890	
   891	    // SAFETY: Safe because variants is guaranteed to contain exactly 3 entries:
   892	    // * most flat
   893	    // * middle
   894	    // * most expanded
   895	    // ... and best fitting only requires the most flat/and expanded.
   896	    unsafe {
   897	        f.write_element(FormatElement::BestFitting(
   898	            format_element::BestFittingElement::from_vec_unchecked(variants),
   899	        ));
   900	    }

fn has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(expression: &Expression<'"'"'_>, f: &Formatter<'"'"'_, '"'"'_>) -> bool {
    let comments = f.comments().comments_before(expression.span().start);
    let Some(comment) = comments.last() else {
        return false;
    };

    f.comments().is_type_cast_comment(comment) && !comment.followed_by_newline()
}

   712	    let AstNodes::ExpressionStatement(stmt) = body.statements().first().unwrap().as_ast_nodes()
   713	    else {

    /// Finds the index of a type cast comment before the given span.
    ///
    /// Searches for a JSDoc comment containing @type or @satisfies that is followed
    /// by an opening parenthesis, which indicates a type cast pattern.
    pub fn get_type_cast_comment_index(&self, span: Span) -> Option<usize> {
        self.unprinted_comments().iter().take_while(|c| c.span.end <= span.start).position(
            |comment| {
                self.source_text.next_non_whitespace_byte_is(comment.span.end, b'(')
                    && self.is_type_cast_comment(comment)
            },
        )
    }

    /// Marks the given span as a type cast node.
    pub fn mark_as_type_cast_node(&mut self, node: &impl GetSpan) {
        self.type_cast_node_span = node.span();
        self.last_handled_type_cast_comment = self.printed_count;
    }

    /// Checks if the most recently printed type cast comment has been handled.
    pub fn is_handled_type_cast_comment(&self) -> bool {
        self.printed_count == self.last_handled_type_cast_comment
    }

    #[inline]
    pub fn is_type_cast_node(&self, node: &impl GetSpan) -> bool {
        self.type_cast_node_span == node.span()
    }

  1573	impl<'a> Format<'a> for AstNode<'a, ParenthesizedExpression<'a>> {
  1574	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>) {
  1575	        let is_suppressed = f.comments().is_suppressed(self.span().start);
  1576	        if !is_suppressed && format_type_cast_comment_node(self, false, f) {
  1577	            return;
  1578	        }
  1579	        self.format_leading_comments(f);
  1580	        let needs_parentheses = self.needs_parentheses(f);
  1581	        if needs_parentheses {
  1582	            "(".fmt(f);
  1583	        }
  1584	        if is_suppressed {
  1585	            FormatSuppressedNode(self.span()).fmt(f);
  1586	        } else {

   431	
   432	impl<'a> FormatWrite<'a> for AstNode<'a, ChainExpression<'a>> {
   433	    fn write(&self, f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>) {
   434	        // When ChainExpression contains TSNonNullExpression, we print `(a?.b)!` instead of `(a?.b!)`
   435	        // This normalizes `(a?.b!).c` to `(a?.b)!.c` to match Prettier's output.
   436	        // See: https://github.com/prettier/prettier/blob/main/src/language-js/clean.js
   437	        if let AstNodes::TSNonNullExpression(non_null) = self.expression().as_ast_nodes() {
   438	            let needs_parens =
   439	                crate::parentheses::chain_expression_needs_parens(self.span, self.parent());
   440	            if needs_parens {
   441	                write!(f, "(");
   442	            }
   443	            non_null.expression().fmt(f);
   444	            if needs_parens {
   445	                write!(f, ")");
   446	            }
   447	            write!(f, "!");
   448	        } else {
   449	            self.expression().fmt(f);
   450	        }
   451	    }
   452	}
   453	
   454	impl<'a> FormatWrite<'a> for AstNode<'a, ParenthesizedExpression<'a>> {
   455	    fn write(&self, _f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>) {
   456	        unreachable!("No `ParenthesizedExpression` as we disabled `preserve_parens` in the parser")
   457	    }
   458	}
   459	
   460	impl<'a> FormatWrite<'a> for AstNode<'a, EmptyStatement> {
   461	    fn write(&self, f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>) {
   462	        if matches!(
   463	            self.parent(),
   464	            AstNodes::DoWhileStatement(_)
   465	                | AstNodes::IfStatement(_)
   466	                | AstNodes::WhileStatement(_)
   467	                | AstNodes::ForStatement(_)
   468	                | AstNodes::ForInStatement(_)
   469	                | AstNodes::ForOfStatement(_)
   470	                | AstNodes::WithStatement(_)
   471	        ) {
   472	            write!(f, ";");
   473	        }
   474	    }

    #[inline]
    pub fn body(&self) -> &AstNode<'a, FunctionBody<'a>> {
        let following_span_start = self.following_span_start;
        self.allocator.alloc(AstNode {
            inner: self.inner.body.as_ref(),
            allocator: self.allocator,
            parent: AstNodes::ArrowFunctionExpression(transmute_self(self)),
            following_span_start,
        })
    }

    #[inline]
    pub fn pure(&self) -> bool {
        self.inner.pure
    }

    #[inline]
    pub fn pife(&self) -> bool {
        self.inner.pife
    }

    pub fn format_leading_comments(&self, f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>) {
        format_leading_comments(self.span()).fmt(f);
    }

    pub fn format_trailing_comments(&self, f: &mut Formatter<'_, 'a>) {
        format_trailing_comments(self.parent.span(), self.inner.span(), self.following_span_start)
            .fmt(f);
    }
}

   141	                // Therefore if our body is an arrow self, array, or object, we

   143	                // going to get broken anyways.
   144	                let arrow_expression = arrow.get_expression();
   145	
   146	                if let Some(expression @ Expression::SequenceExpression(sequence)) =
   147	                    arrow_expression
   148	                    && !has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(expression, f)
   149	                {
   150	                    return if let Some(format_sequence) =
   151	                        format_sequence_with_leading_comment(sequence.span(), &format_body, f)
   152	                    {
   153	                        write!(f, [group(&format_args!(formatted_signature, format_sequence))]);

   168	                }
   169	
   170	                write!(f, formatted_signature);
   171	
   172	                let body_has_soft_line_break =
   173	                    arrow_expression.is_none_or(|expression| match expression {
   174	                        Expression::ArrowFunctionExpression(_)
   175	                        | Expression::ArrayExpression(_)
   176	                        | Expression::ObjectExpression(_) => {
   177	                            !f.comments().has_leading_own_line_comment(body.span().start)

+pub fn arrow_function_body_has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(
+    arrow_function: &ArrowFunctionExpression<'_>,
+    f: &Formatter<'_, '_>,
+) -> bool {
+    arrow_function
+        .get_expression()
+        .is_some_and(|expression| has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(expression, f))
+}
+
+fn has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(
+    expression: &Expression<'_>,
+    f: &Formatter<'_, '_>,
+) -> bool {
+    let comment = if let Some(type_cast_comments) = is_type_cast_node(expression, f) {
+        type_cast_comments.last().or_else(|| f.comments().printed_comments().last())
+    } else if f.comments().is_type_cast_node(expression) {
+        f.comments().printed_comments().last()
+    } else {
+        None
+    };
+
+    comment.is_some_and(|comment| !comment.followed_by_newline())
+}
+
 fn has_rest_object_or_array_parameter(params: &FormalParameters) -> bool {
     params.rest.is_some()
         || params.items.iter().any(|param| param.pattern.is_destructuring_pattern())

+pub fn arrow_function_body_has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(
+    arrow_function: &ArrowFunctionExpression<'_>,
+    f: &Formatter<'_, '_>,
+) -> bool {
+    arrow_function
+        .get_expression()
+        .is_some_and(|expression| has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(expression, f))
+}
+
+fn has_leading_inline_type_cast_comment(
+    expression: &Expression<'_>,
+    f: &Formatter<'_, '_>,
+) -> bool {
+    let comment = if let Some(type_cast_comments) = is_type_cast_node(expression, f) {
+        type_cast_comments.last().or_else(|| f.comments().printed_comments().last())
+    } else if f.comments().is_type_cast_node(expression) {
+        f.comments().printed_comments().last()
+    } else {
+        None
+    };
+
+    comment.is_some_and(|comment| !comment.followed_by_newline())
+}
+
 fn has_rest_object_or_array_parameter(params: &FormalParameters) -> bool {
     params.rest.is_some()
         || params.items.iter().any(|param| param.pattern.is_destructuring_pattern())
